+    befores = INVALID_HOOKS_DEFINITION_TEMPLATE['before']
+    events = INVALID_HOOKS_DEFINITION_TEMPLATE['events']

+        befores[0]['run']
+        .replace('{name}', name.upper())
+        .replace('{type}', type.upper())

+    befores[1]['run'] = (
+        befores[1]['run']
+        .replace('{name}', name.upper())
+        .replace('{type}', type.upper())
+    )
+    if type == 'PROVIDER':
+        events.append({'category': '_'})
+    elif type == 'CHANNEL':
+        events.append({'channel': 'setup'})
